I = imread('Cat.jpg');
J = rgb2gray(I);
[r, c] = size(J);
s = r*c;
h = zeros(1, 256);
z = zeros(1, 300);

for i = 1:r
for j = 1:c
    t = J(i,j);
h(t) = h(t)+1;
end
end
pdf = h/s;
cdf(1) = pdf(1);
for i = 2:256
cdf(i) = cdf(i-1)+pdf(i)
end
new = round(cdf*256);
new = new+1;
for i=1:r
for j=1:c
temp = J(i,j);
b(i,j) = new(temp);
t = b(i,j);
z(t) = z(t)+1;
end
end
b=b-1;
subplot(2,2,1), imshow(J);
title('Gray image');
subplot(2,2,2), bar(h, 'b');
title('Histogram calculated');
subplot(2,2,3), imshow(uint8(b));
title('Emhanced image calculated');
subplot(2,2,4), bar(z, 'b');
title('Histogram calculated for Enhanced image');
